< Review>
Perfect for all families, comedy fans, and friends out for a night on the town. Fast-paced and vibrant, the performers of Comedy Sportz bring alive an improvised comedy show built from suggestions given by the audience. The short-form structure (short games, scenes, and competitions) means that you could even walk in late immediately be brought up to speed. The performers are some of the most seasoned and passionate in all of Los Angeles. You can feel that everyone there loves what they do. Every weekend they bring joy and laughter to new fans, come join them!</Review>

< review>
This is the only comedy club I have found so far that is all "clean jokes". Perfect place to bring your kids with you.

I love their improv, all the performers are very talented. They offer classes too!

No drinks minimum required. They do sell drinks/snacks at the back of the theater. Nice seating area during intermission.<//review>

<review>We have seen many shows at The ComedySportz Theater and have always left there with our sides aching from laughing so hard! We have seen the College Team matches, The Professional Team matches and several long form improv shows. It's hard to say which is our favorite. Chickspeare, the Resistance, and Manor House Manner are all hysterical and fun. Everyone is friendly (and funny), and the actors come out after the shows to greet the audience. They are amazing! We order our tickets ahead of time to save a couple bucks.  A night out at the CSz Theater is really a hoot!< /review>< pictures>

< date>
1561916985653< /date>
<rate>5<//rate>< Text>
If you want a whale watching adventure or just an exciting ride around the harbor I highly recommend SLO tours out of Port San Luis pier in Avila Beach. This is our second time going out with Captain Michael Brink and we will definitely go again.  This is not a slow trolling experience - It is a very fast ride on a coast guard Zodiac style boat, but I felt totally safe the whole time (and I can't swim!).  If you sit outside prepare to get quite wet (exhilarating), but the enclosed area is perfect for those who prefer to stay dry.  Captain Michael is amazing at navigating to where the whales are hanging out.  I'd like to take his Ocean Rafting tour as well to explore the coastline and enjoy the roller coaster of a ride.  It is really worth the price to book with SLO tours.</Text>

Customer service here is top notch especially the lady boss/cashier. I've been a few times and she always has a sweet welcoming presence. She might be the sole reason some people frequent this place because she adds such a highlight to anyone's day.
The food itself is quite tasty. Typical Chinese cuisine, the usually well seasoned but I did had a very bland order one time I came. The portion sizes are great and the prices are quite cheap.
The restaurant usually isn't very crowded n tucked away in a business Park so it's a nice place to eat with a large group or even just sit in for a bite alone. No need to feel pressured to drag along a buddy. I reccomend giving this place a try if your in the area looking for some convenient Chinese food.< /Text>

<UserId.>100370880834218092676</UserId.><name>Shantala Shenoy<//name>< time>

<Rating>4< /Rating>< review>
We came across this restaurant while we were on a long drive across California. And to be honest this place was a pretty random pick, as we were super hungry at that point (when we found this joint) and were willing to stop at the first Indian restaurant with half decent reviews.

So all that considered, we were quite lucky that this was actually a pretty good place with really tasty food. We ordered Tandoori Fish Koliwada & Chicken Biriyani here, and both those dishes were delicious.

Though I've to say that the Fish Koliwada was nothing like we expected a Koliwada dish to be. Because traditionally Koliwada is a fried fish preparation and this was baked. So that was a disappointment, but the fish still tasted good, so overall it was okay.<//review>

<Rating>4</Rating><text>Goan grub makes for Namaste Nom-Nom's

Mandovi Indian Cuisine specializes in cuisine from Goa, located in Western India.  Goa was colonized by the Portugeuse, whom heavily influenced the culture & taste of the region.

I attended a special weekend lunch buffet, which is normally available during weekdays only.

There was a myriad of offerings beautifully displayed on the buffet line.  Selections such as-

Tandoori wings & fried fish

Biryani rice & curry puffs

I brought my appetite, having 3 loaded plates of spicy deliciousness

The highlights for me were the butter chicken, fried fish & biryani rice.  The butter chicken was tender & buttery rich.  The fried fish was flaky w/o being oily.  Lastly, the biryani rice was fluffy & moist.  I didn't mind loading up on carbs on this occasion.

Don't forget the desserts!  I satiated my sweet tooth with kheer, fresh fruit & chocolate dipped strawberries
The health benefits of strawberries w/ the pleasing taste of chocolate.  A romantic way to feed your tablemates ;p

For an additional charge, my table opted for ghulab jamun
Fried doughballs doused in syrup, these are a great way to bust your diet.  Sweet & pleasing to the tastebuds, the ghulab jamun are not to be passed up.

Service was great.  We were promptly attended to, with our drinks being refilled & plates being cleared whenever needed.  Plenty of table seating for large or small groups.  Parking is in a private lot shared by The Boat, Togo's and other businesses.

We all left with full bellies from Delhi.

Mandovi Indian Cuisine offers authentic Goan cuisine that'll spice up your day.  I live very close to Little India, so I normally frequent restaurants there, but if I was in the South Bay area, then I wouldn't hesitate paying a visit to Mandovi for some spice-laden chow.

Highly recommend!

<Review>Employees don't do anything to upkeep the gym! Everything is dirty all the time. 80% of Treadmills don't work properly.The gym Equipment is never disinfected!! ------------------------------------------------------BE CAREFUL!------------------------------------------
STAPHYLOCOCCUS AUREUS----------------------
What is it?
Staphylococcus aureus, commonly known as staph, is a bacteria that mostly causes skin infections.
Symptoms-
Staph infections are usually mild and include superficial rashes, pimples and/or boils on your skin. However, if the bacteria spreads and gets deeper into your skin, it can become a life-threatening infection such as pneumonia, sepsis or meningitis. Recently there have been reports of MRSA (methicillin-resistant Staphylococcus aureus), a very aggressive form of Staph that's resistant to antibiotics, in gyms, but it's extremely rare.
How do you get it?
It's spread through contact, so it can be picked up through a shared towel or razor, exercise equipment surfaces and grips or skin-to-skin contact.
How do you treat it?
A course of antibiotics should do the trick.

-------------CANDIDA---------------------
What is it?
The most common culprit in fungal infections, this yeast-like fungus can lead to everything from athlete's foot to ringworm to jock itch in men and yeast infections in women.
How do you get it?
Contact. It loves warm, moist areas, so locker rooms, saunas, swimming pools and showers are the perfect environment to pick up some tasty foot fungus.
Symptoms-
Ringworm is usually marked by ring-shaped skin rashes, usually on your toes, sometimes on your palms and between your fingers. Athlete's foot gives you itchy, cracked, flaking and peeling skin between the toes or side of the foot, while jock itch causes a rash on your groin. If it's untreated, it can escalate to blisters and severely cracked skin.
How do you treat it?
Antifungal creams, but if it escalates into an infection, antibiotics will do the trick.
-----------STREPTOCOCCAL BACTERIA--------------------------
What is it?
A type of bacteria that usually causes upper respiratory infections--strep throat. There are 20 different types of strep bacteria.
How do you get it?
It's very contagious and is spread through person-to-person contact, airborne droplets, doorknobs and other surfaces. Sweaty exercise equipment, saunas, locker rooms and drinking bottles can harbor strep.
Symptoms-
Symptoms can range from mild throat infections to pneumonia. It can also cause skin infections such as impetigo, which causes blisters, and cellulitis, which affects deeper layers of skin.
How do you treat it?
Antibiotics, although minor strep infections, such as a throat and inner ear infections, usually get better on their own. Skin infections are treated with antibiotic tablets or creams, and more serious infections like pneumonia and meningitis require hospitalization and intravenous antibiotics.</Review>< userid>
